\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l00054}00054 \textcolor{comment}{  /// A Generalised Element class.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l00055}00055 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l00056}00056 \textcolor{comment}{  /// The main components of a GeneralisedElement are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l00057}00057 \textcolor{comment}{  /// -\/ pointers to its internal and external Data, which are stored together}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l00058}00058 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   in a single array so that we need only store one pointer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l00059}00059 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   The internal Data are placed at the beginning}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l00060}00060 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   of the array and the external Data are stored at the end.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l00061}00061 \textcolor{comment}{  /// -\/ a pointer to a global Time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l00062}00062 \textcolor{comment}{  /// -\/ a lookup table that establishes the relation between local}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l00063}00063 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   and global equation numbers.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l00064}00064 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l00065}00065 \textcolor{comment}{  /// We also provide interfaces for functions that compute the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l00066}00066 \textcolor{comment}{  /// element's Jacobian matrix and/or the Vector of residuals.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l00067}00067 \textcolor{comment}{  /// In addition, an interface that returns a mass matrix -\/-\/-\/ the matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l00068}00068 \textcolor{comment}{  /// of terms that multiply any time derivatives in the problem -\/-\/-\/ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l00069}00069 \textcolor{comment}{  /// also provided to permit explicit time-\/stepping and the solution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l00070}00070 \textcolor{comment}{  /// of the generalised eigenproblems.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l03550}03550 \textcolor{comment}{  /// in the Jacobian matrix, are determined by finite differencing.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l04990}04990 \textcolor{comment}{  /// FaceGeometry class definition: This policy class is used to allow}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l04991}04991 \textcolor{comment}{  /// construction of face elements that solve arbitrary equations without}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l04992}04992 \textcolor{comment}{  /// having to tamper with the corresponding "{}bulk"{} elements.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{elements_8h_source_l04993}04993 \textcolor{comment}{  /// The geometrical information for the face element must be specified}}
